85127 - Crimson Harvest Expert System <font size="14">Crimson Harvest Expert System</font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly T1 battlecruisers.

The temporary skills provided by this Expert System last for seven days.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active rental period. As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 Standard Expert Systems

85242 - Hypercatabolic Clone Tissue This human genetic material shows signs of extreme modification previously only observed in Jovian samples.

Genetic modeling extrapolates that a clone grown from this sample would have a metabolic rate a hundred times higher, produce ten times as much adrenaline, and have a drastically lower reaction time. It is however incredibly unstable, and would likely die before taking its first breath.

725107 Tetrimon Tetrimon
725108 The Order of St. Tetrimon is an Amarr religious order known for its fanatical followers and radical scriptural, theocratic, and militarist doctrines. The Order is named for St. Tetrimon, an Ardishapur noble who assassinated his grandfather the Emperor Zaragram II, in response to the increasingly megalomaniac and heretical actions of the "Mad Emperor". The Order of St. Tetrimon is an Amarr religious order known for its fanatical followers and radical scriptural, theocratic, and militarist doctrines. The Order is named for St. Tetrimon, an Ardishapur noble who assassinated his grandfather the Emperor Zaragram II, in response to the increasingly megalomaniac and heretical actions of the "Mad Emperor".

725111 Blood Raiders: Crimson Harvest Blood Raiders: Crimson Harvest
725112 Blood Raiders Blood Raiders
725113 The Blood Raider Covenant is a particularly gruesome sect of Sani Sabik cult. While all modern Sani Sabik rituals use blood in some manner or another, the Blood Raiders Covenant places particular value on it, and will go to great lengths to acquire it from what they believe to be the richest and most unspoiled sources. They are considered among the most dangerous and depraved of all pirate elements operating in space. The Blood Raider Covenant is a particularly gruesome sect of Sani Sabik cult. 726931 Crimson Harvest Expert System Crimson Harvest Expert System Name of item 85127 (Standard Expert Systems)
726932 <font size="14">Crimson Harvest Expert System</font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly T1 battlecruisers.

The temporary skills provided by this Expert System last for seven days.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active rental period. As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 <font size="14"><b>Crimson Harvest Expert System</b></font>
